Trump cards can be used to conquer other cards when no more cards of the same suit are there to offer. diagonal.\r\n- The queen moves to any distance vertically, horizontally or diagonally.\r\n- The rook moves to any distance vertically or horizontally.\r\n- The knight moves to the field, which is in king.\r\n\r\n- Check - the situation in chess, when a king is under immediate attack by opponent's pieces\r\n- Checkmate - the situation in chess, when the player whose turn it is to move is in check
